\DoxyCodeLine{00290\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00291\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Vector\ types\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00292\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00293\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ Note:\ \ \ OpenCL\ requires\ that\ all\ types\ be\ naturally\ aligned.\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00294\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ This\ means\ that\ vector\ types\ must\ be\ naturally\ aligned.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00295\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ For\ example,\ a\ vector\ of\ four\ floats\ must\ be\ aligned\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00296\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ a\ 16\ byte\ boundary\ (calculated\ as\ 4\ *\ the\ natural\ 4-\/byte\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00297\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ alignment\ of\ the\ float).\ \ The\ alignment\ qualifiers\ here}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00298\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ will\ only\ function\ properly\ if\ your\ compiler\ supports\ them}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00299\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ and\ if\ you\ don't\ actively\ work\ to\ defeat\ them.\ \ For\ example,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00300\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ in\ order\ for\ a\ cl\_float4\ to\ be\ 16\ byte\ aligned\ in\ a\ struct,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00301\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ the\ start\ of\ the\ struct\ must\ itself\ be\ 16-\/byte\ aligned.\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00302\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00303\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Maintaining\ proper\ alignment\ is\ the\ user's\ responsibility.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00304\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01538\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ Each\ line\ thereafter\ of\ OpenCL\ C\ source\ must\ end\ with:\ \(\backslash\)n\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01539\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ The\ last\ line\ ends\ in\ "{};}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01540\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01541\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ Example:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01542\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01543\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ const\ char\ *my\_program\ =\ CL\_PROGRAM\_STRING\_BEGIN\ "{}\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01544\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ kernel\ void\ foo(\ int\ a,\ float\ *\ b\ )\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \(\backslash\)n\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01545\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \(\backslash\)n\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01546\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ //\ my\ comment\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \(\backslash\)n\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01547\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ *b[\ get\_global\_id(0)]\ =\ a;\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \(\backslash\)n\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01548\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \(\backslash\)n\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01549\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ "{};}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01550\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01551\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ should\ correctly\ set\ up\ the\ line,\ (column)\ and\ file\ information\ for\ your\ source\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{01552\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ string\ so\ you\ can\ do\ source\ level\ debugging.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01553\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01554\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ \_\_CL\_STRINGIFY(\_x)\ \#\_x}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01555\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ \_CL\_STRINGIFY(\_x)\ \_\_CL\_STRINGIFY(\_x)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01556\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ CL\_PROGRAM\_STRING\_DEBUG\_INFO\ "{}\#line\ "{}\ \_CL\_STRINGIFY(\_\_LINE\_\_)\ "{}\ \(\backslash\)"{}"{}\ \_\_FILE\_\_\ "{}\(\backslash\)"{}\ \(\backslash\)n\(\backslash\)n"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01557\ }
